The plough (<b>LƒÅ·πÖgala, Sƒ´ra</b>) was drawn by oxen, teams of six, eight, or even twelve being employed.<sup>10</sup> The operations of agriculture are neatly summed up in the ≈öatapatha BrƒÅhma·πáa<sup>11</sup> as ‚Äòploughing, sowing, reaping, and threshing‚Äô (<i>k·πõ·π£anta·∏•,</i> <i>vapanta·∏•, lunanta·∏•, m·πõ·πáanta·∏•</i>).
